5  리스트(list), 파일 입출력 그리고 CSV

5.1 멜론 top100(v1) - 함수와 리스트를 사용한 CSV 파일 처리

def data_loading(filename):
    f = open(filename, "r", encoding="utf-8")
    top100 = []
    f.readline()
    for i in f.readlines():
        top100.append(i.strip().split(","))
    f.close()
    return top100

def get_artist_names(data):
    artists = []
    for song in data:
        if song[3] not in artists:
            artists.append(song[3])
    return artists

def find_song_id(data, artist_name):
    ids = []
    for i in data:
        if (
            i[3].replace(" ", "").lower().find(artist_name.replace(" ", "").lower())
            != -1
        ):
            ids.append(i[0])
    return ids

def find_song_info(data, song_id):
    for i in data:
        if i[0] == str(song_id):
            return i
    return None

def count_all_song(data):
    artists = []
    for row in data:
        if row[3] not in artists:
            artists.append(row[3])
    artists_count = {}
    for artist in artists:
        m = 0
        artists_count[artist] = 0
        for row in data:
            if artist == row[3]:
                artists_count[artist] += 1
    return artists_count

if __name__ == "__main__":
    top100 = data_loading("data/melon-top100.csv")
    print("get_artist_names : ", get_artist_names(top100[0:5]))
    song_id = find_song_id(top100, "임영웅")
    print("song_id : ", song_id)
    song_info = find_song_info(top100, song_id[0])
    print("song_info : ", song_info)
    print("count_all_song : ", count_all_song(top100))

5.2 멜론 top100(v2) - 함수, 딕셔너리 그리고 모듈을 사용한 CSV 파일 처리

import csv

def data_loading(filename):
    with open(filename, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f)
        result = list(reader)
    return result

def get_artist_names(data):
    artists = {}
    for song in data:
        artists[song["artist"]] = None
    return list(artists.keys())

def find_song_id(data, artist_name):
    ids = []
    artist_name = artist_name.replace(" ", "").lower()
    for row in data:
        if (
            row["artist"].replace(" ", "").lower().find(artist_name.replace(" ", "").lower())
            != -1
        ):
            ids.append(row["song_no"])
    return ids

def find_song_info(data, song_id):
    infos = []
    for song in data:
        if  song_id == song["song_no"]:
            return song
        
def count_all_song(data):
    count_song = {}
    for song in top100:
        if song["artist"] not in count_song:
            count_song[song["artist"]] = 1
        else:
            count_song[song["artist"]] += 1
    return count_song

if __name__ == "__main__":
    top100 = data_loading("data/melon-top100.csv")
    print("get_artist_names : ", get_artist_names(top100[0:5]))
    song_id = find_song_id(top100, "임영웅")
    print("song_id : ", song_id)
    song_info = find_song_info(top100, song_id[0])
    print("song_info : ", song_info)
    print("count_all_song : ", count_all_song(top100))

5.3 멜론 top100(v3) - Collections을 사용한 CSV 파일 처리

import csv
from collections import Counter

def data_loading(filename):
    with open(filename, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f)
        result = list(reader)
    return result

def get_artist_names(data):
    return [{song["artist"] for song in data}]

def find_song_id(data, artist_name):
    is_find = lambda x: x.replace(" ", "").lower().find(artist_name.replace(" ", "").lower())
    ids = [song["song_no"] for song in data if is_find(song["artist"]) != -1]
    return ids

def find_song_info(data, song_id):
    return [song for song in data if song["song_no"] == song_id]

def count_all_song(data):
    artists = [song["artist"] for song in data]
    return Counter(artists)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    top100 = data_loading("data/melon-top100.csv")
    print("get_artist_names : ", get_artist_names(top100[0:5]))
    song_id = find_song_id(top100, "임영웅")
    print("song_id : ", song_id)
    song_info = find_song_info(top100, song_id[0])
    print("song_info : ", song_info)
    print("count_all_song : ", count_all_song(top100))

song_id :  ['34061322', '34908740', '35008524', '35834583', '35834584', '32508053', '35008525', '35008527', '35008528', '35008534', '35008526', '35008531', '35008532', '35008530']

6 과제3(a) - 빌보드 차트

  • Assignment03a
import csv
from datetime import datetime
from collections import defaultdict
from collections import Counter
import re

def read_csv_to_dict(filename="assignment03.csv"):
    with open(filename, 'r', encoding='utf8') as file:
        csv_reader = csv.DictReader(file)
        return list(csv_reader)

billboard = read_csv_to_dict("data/billboard_hot100.csv")

def unique_songs(csv_reader):
    unique_songs = set()
    for row in csv_reader:
        unique_songs.add(row['title'])
    unique_song_list = sorted(unique_songs)
    return unique_song_list

print("unique_songs : ", unique_songs(billboard))

def singer_rank(csv_reader):
    performer_stats = defaultdict(lambda: {'count': 0, 'earliest_year': float('inf')})
    for row in csv_reader:
        if int(row['peak_pos']) == 1:
            performer = row['performer']
            year = datetime.strptime(row['chart_week'], '%Y-%m-%d').year
            performer_stats[performer]['count'] += 1
            if year < performer_stats[performer]['earliest_year']:
                performer_stats[performer]['earliest_year'] = year

    performers_list = [(performer, stats['count'], stats['earliest_year']) for performer, stats in performer_stats.items()]
    sorted_performers = sorted(performers_list, key=lambda x: (-x[1], x[2]))
    return sorted_performers

for performer, count, year in singer_rank(billboard)[0:1]:    
    print(f"singer_rank : {performer}, {count} #1s, Earliest Year: {year}")    

def clean_and_split_title(title):
    cleaned_title = re.sub(r'[^\w\s]', '', title)
    return cleaned_title.lower().split()

def word_frequencies(csv_reader):    
    word_frequencies = Counter()
    for row in csv_reader:
        title = row['title']
        words = clean_and_split_title(title)
        word_frequencies.update(words)
    sorted_word_frequencies = sorted(word_frequencies.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
    return sorted_word_frequencies

print("word_frequencies", word_frequencies(billboard)[0:5])

def longest_charting_songs(csv_reader):
    longest_charting_songs_per_year = {}
    for row in csv_reader:
        year = datetime.strptime(row['chart_week'], '%Y-%m-%d').year
        weeks_on_chart = int(row['wks_on_chart'])
        if year not in longest_charting_songs_per_year:
            longest_charting_songs_per_year[year] = {'title': row['title'], 'weeks': weeks_on_chart}
        else:
            if weeks_on_chart > longest_charting_songs_per_year[year]['weeks']:
                longest_charting_songs_per_year[year] = {'title': row['title'], 'weeks': weeks_on_chart}
    sorted_years = sorted(longest_charting_songs_per_year.keys())
    years_song_info = [(year, longest_charting_songs_per_year[year]) for year in sorted_years]
    return years_song_info

print("longest_charting_songs : ", longest_charting_songs(billboard)[-1])
